<a name="_bclHeader1"></a><DIV>
<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; MARGIN: 12pt 0pt 0pt 0cm" align=center>
<IMG src="x14121222430100.jpg" width=794 height=169>&nbsp;</P></DIV>
<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; MARGIN: 0cm 7.1pt 0pt 0cm" align=center><B><FONT 
style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt" lang=EN-US face="arial narrow,sans-
serif"></FONT></B>&nbsp;</P>
<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; MARGIN: 12pt 0pt 0pt 0cm" align=center><B><FONT 
style="FONT-SIZE: 16pt" lang=EN-US color=black face="arial narrow,sans-
serif">Third Quarter 2014 Condensed Information</FONT></B></P>
<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0cm 0pt 0pt 0cm"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 
11pt" lang=EN-US color=black face="arial narrow,sans-serif"></FONT>&nbsp;</P>
<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0cm 0pt 0pt 0cm"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 
11pt" lang=EN-US color=black face="arial narrow,sans-serif">Rio de Janeiro, 
December 12, 2014 &#8211; Petr&#243;leo Brasileiro S.A. &#8211; Petrobras 
announces that today, in light of new facts that occurred after November 13, 
2014, directly or indirectly related to the &#8220;Lava Jato Operation&#8221;, 
it decided not to file its consolidated interim financial statements for the 
3<SUP>rd</SUP> quarter 2014 not reviewed by the independent auditors. These 
facts are set out below:</FONT></P>
<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0cm 0pt 0pt 0cm"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 
11pt" lang=EN-US color=black face="arial narrow,sans-serif"></FONT>&nbsp;</P>
<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0cm 0pt"><FONT 
style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt" lang=EN-US color=black face="arial narrow,sans-serif">
<TABLE style="WIDTH: 100%" border=0 cellSpacing=0 cellPadding=0>
<TR>
<TD vAlign=top width="3%"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt" lang=EN-US 
color=#000000 face="arial narrow,sans-serif">(i)<SUP>&nbsp;</SUP></FONT></TD>
<TD vAlign=top width="97%">
<P align=justify><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt" lang=EN-US color=#000000 
face="arial narrow,sans-serif">Obtained a waiver for its earliest financial 
reporting covenants that allows the Company to release its interim financial 
statements for the 3<SUP>rd</SUP> quarter 2014 by January 31, 2015, with no risk
of acceleration of its finance debt by its creditors;</FONT></P></TD></TR>
<TR>
<TD vAlign=top width="3%"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt" lang=EN-US 
color=#000000 face="arial narrow,sans-serif">(ii)</FONT><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 
7pt" lang=EN-US color=#000000 face="times new roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD vAlign=top width="97%">
<P align=justify><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt" lang=EN-US color=#000000 
face="arial narrow,sans-serif">On November 21, 2014, Petrobras received a 
subpoena from the U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission (SEC) requesting 
certain documents relating to an investigation of the Company by the 
SEC;</FONT></P></TD></TR>
<TR>
<TD vAlign=top width="3%"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt" lang=EN-US 
color=#000000 face="arial narrow,sans-serif">(iii)</FONT><FONT style="FONT-SIZE:
7pt" lang=EN-US color=#000000 face="times new roman">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD vAlign=top width="97%">
<P align=justify><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt" lang=EN-US color=#000000 
face="arial narrow,sans-serif">On December 3, 2014, Petrobras gained access to 
the depositions of Mr. Julio Gerin de Almeida Camargo (Grupo Toyo) and Mr. 
Augusto Ribeiro de Mendon&#231;a Neto (Grupo Setal) given as state&#8217;s 
evidence to prosecutors;</FONT></P></TD></TR>
<TR>
<TD vAlign=top width="3%"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt" lang=EN-US 
color=#000000 face="arial narrow,sans-serif">(iv)</FONT><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 
7pt" lang=EN-US color=#000000 face="times new 
roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD vAlign=top width="97%">
<P align=justify><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt" lang=EN-US color=#000000 
face="arial narrow,sans-serif">On December 9, 2014, the Company was served with 
a class-action complaint filed by Mr. Peter Kaltman before the U.S. Court 
(United States District Court, Southern District of New York). We expect 
additional complaints to be filed, which could potentially be consolidated with 
Kaltman&#8217;s complaint;</FONT></P></TD></TR>
<TR>
<TD vAlign=top width="3%"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt" lang=EN-US 
color=#000000 face="arial narrow,sans-serif">(v)</FONT><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 
7pt" lang=EN-US color=#000000 face="times new 
roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD vAlign=top width="97%">
<P align=justify><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt" lang=EN-US color=#000000 
face="arial narrow,sans-serif">On November 11, 2014, criminal charges were filed
by the Brazilian Public Prosecutor&#8217;s Office against several individuals, 
including the Former Director of Downstream, Paulo Roberto Costa, and managers 
of other companies for active corruption, passive corruption, organized crime, 
money-laundering and falsification of 
documents.</FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE></FONT><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt" 
lang=EN-US color=black face="arial narrow,sans-serif"></FONT></P>
<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0cm 0pt 0pt 0cm"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 
11pt" lang=EN-US color=black face="arial narrow,sans-serif"></FONT>&nbsp;</P>
<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0cm 0pt 0pt 0cm"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 
11pt" lang=EN-US color=black face="arial narrow,sans-serif">However, in order to
comply with its responsibility to inform and to foster diligence and 
transparency the Company is releasing information regarding its operational 
performance and certain other financial information that Petrobras believes 
would not be affected by the potential adjustments to its financial statements 
resulting from the &#8220;Lava Jato Operation&#8221;. This information has not 
been reviewed by our independent auditors.</FONT></P>
<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0cm 0pt 0pt 0cm"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 
11pt" lang=EN-US color=black face="arial narrow,sans-serif"></FONT>&nbsp;</P>
<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; MARGIN: 0cm 0pt 0pt 0cm" align=center><FONT 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt" lang=EN-US face="arial narrow,sans-
serif"></FONT>&nbsp;</P>
<DIV align=right>

<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; MARGIN: 0cm 0pt 0pt 0cm" align=center><FONT 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt" lang=EN-US face="arial narrow,sans-
serif"></FONT>&nbsp;</P>
<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0cm 0pt 0pt 0cm"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 
11pt" lang=EN-US face="arial narrow,sans-serif"></FONT>&nbsp;</P>
<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0cm 0pt 0pt 0cm"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 
11pt" lang=EN-US face="arial narrow,sans-serif">Sales Revenues reached R$ 88,378
million and Cash and Cash Equivalents reached R$ 62,409 million in the 3Q-2014. 
</FONT></P>
<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0cm 0pt 0pt 0cm"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 
11pt" lang=EN-US face="arial narrow,sans-serif"></FONT>&nbsp;</P>
<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0cm 0pt 0pt 0cm"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 
11pt" lang=EN-US face="arial narrow,sans-serif">Sales revenues were 7% higher 
when compared to the 2Q-2014, resulting from higher crude oil exports and 
increased domestic demand, mainly diesel, which was mostly met by domestic 
output of oil products. When compared to Jan-Sep/2013, the 13% increase in sales
revenues is attributable to higher oil product prices in the domestic market 
resulting from the impact in the full year of 2014 of diesel and gasoline price 
adjustments in 2013 and the impact of foreign currency depreciation (8%) over 
the price of oil products that are adjusted to reflect international prices and 
export prices, as well as higher electricity and natural gas prices. Domestic 
demand for </FONT>
<FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt" lang=EN-US face="arial narrow,sans-serif">oil 
products increased by 3%, mainly diesel (2%), gasoline (5%) and fuel oil (21%), 
and crude oil exports volume was 12% higher, partially offset by a decrease in 
fuel oil exports volume (14%).</FONT></P>
<a name="_bclFooter1"></a><DIV>
<P style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt" lang=PT-BR 
face="Times New Roman"></FONT>&nbsp;</P></DIV></DIV>
<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: right">1</P>

<DIV style="PADDING-LEFT: 0%; PADDING-RIGHT: 0%">
<a name="_bclHeader2"></a><DIV>
<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; MARGIN: 12pt 0pt 0pt 0cm" align=center>
<IMG src="x14121222430100.jpg" width=794 height=169>&nbsp;</P>
<P style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">&nbsp;</P></DIV>
<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0cm 0pt 0pt 0cm"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 
11pt" lang=EN-US face="arial narrow,sans-serif"></FONT>&nbsp;</P>
<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0cm 0pt 0pt 0cm"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 
11pt" lang=EN-US face="arial narrow,sans-serif">Our Executive Officers recently 
approved the implementation of a series of actions that will be undertaken in 
order to maintain our cash level, which was R$ 62.4 billion as of September 30, 
2014, and the liquidity of the Company. These actions include, for example, 
discounting receivables, reducing the level of capital expenditures, reviewing 
product pricing strategies and reducing operating costs in activities that were 
out of the scope of our structuring cost reduction programs; and assure positive
free cash flow next year, considering crude oil prices of around U.S.$ 70/bbl 
and foreign exchange rate of R$ 2.60/U.S.$; thus eliminating the need for 
additional financing in the capital markets next year.</FONT></P>
<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0cm 0pt 0pt 0cm"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 
11pt" lang=EN-US face="arial narrow,sans-serif"></FONT>&nbsp;</P>

face="Times New Roman"></FONT>&nbsp;</P></DIV></DIV>

<a name="_bclHeader3"></a><DIV>
<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; MARGIN: 12pt 0pt 0pt 0cm" align=center>
<IMG src="x14121222430100.jpg" width=794 height=169>&nbsp;</P>
<P style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 0pt">&nbsp;</P></DIV>
<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt"><B><FONT style="FONT-SIZE:

<TR>
<TD style="PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; 
PADDING-TOP: 0cm" vAlign=top width="49%">
<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 6pt"><B><FONT style="FONT-
SIZE: 9pt" lang=EN-US face="arial narrow,sans-serif">(3Q-2014 x 2Q-
2014):</FONT></B><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 9pt" lang=EN-US face="arial 
narrow,sans-serif"> The 6% increase in crude oil and NGL production is 
attributable to the ramp-up of P-55 (Roncador), P-62 (Roncador), P-58 (Parque 
das Baleias) and FPSO Cidade de Paraty (Lula NE), along with the start-up of the
extended well test of Iara Oeste and of the Anticipated Production System of 
Tartaruga Verde. </FONT></P>
<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 6pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 
9pt" face="arial narrow,sans-serif">Natural gas production increased by 7% due 
to a higher production in P-53 (Marlim Leste), P-54 (Roncador), P-55 (Roncador),
P-62 (Roncador), P-58 (Parque das Baleias), FPSOs Cidade de Santos (Urugu&#225;-
Tamba&#250;) and Cidade de Paraty (Lula NE). </FONT></P>
<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 6pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 
9pt" face="arial narrow,sans-serif"></FONT>&nbsp;</P></TD>
<TD style="PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; 
PADDING-TOP: 0cm" vAlign=top width="2%">
<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 6pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 
9pt" face="arial narrow,sans-serif"></FONT>&nbsp;</P></TD>
<TD style="PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; 
PADDING-TOP: 0cm" vAlign=top width="49%">
<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 6pt"><B><FONT style="FONT-
SIZE: 9pt" lang=EN-US face="arial narrow,sans-serif">(Jan-Sep/2014 x Jan-
Sep/2013):</FONT></B><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 9pt" lang=EN-US face="arial 
narrow,sans-serif"> Crude oil and NGL production increased by 4% in Jan-Sep/2014
resulting from the start-up of Stationary Production Units P-63 (Papa-Terra), P-
55 (Roncador), P-62 (Roncador) and P-58 (Parque das Baleias) and from the ramp-
up of FPSO Cidade de Itaja&#237; (Ba&#250;na), Cidade de Paraty (Lula NE) and 
Cidade de S&#227;o Paulo (Sapinho&#225;). The natural decline of fields 
partially offset these effects.</FONT></P>
<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 6pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 
9pt" lang=EN-US face="arial narrow,sans-serif">The 7% increase in natural gas 
production is attributable to a higher production in Mexilh&#227;o, Parque das 
Baleias, Urugu&#225;-Tamba&#250;, Sapinho&#225; and Lula Nordeste fields. 
</FONT></P>
<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 6pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 
9pt" lang=EN-US face="arial narrow,sans-
serif"></FONT>&nbsp;</P></TD></TR></TABLE></DIV>

<DIV align=right>
<TABLE style="BORDER-BOTTOM: medium none; BORDER-LEFT: medium none; WIDTH: 100%;
BORDER-TOP: medium none; BORDER-RIGHT: medium none" border=0 cellSpacing=0

<TR>
<TD style="PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt;
PADDING-TOP: 0cm" vAlign=top width="49%">
<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 6pt"><B><FONT style="FONT-
SIZE: 9pt" lang=EN-US face="arial narrow,sans-serif">(3Q-2014 x 2Q-
2014):</FONT></B><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 9pt" lang=EN-US face="arial 
narrow,sans-serif"> Our domestic sales volumes increased by 3% when compared to 
the 2Q-2014, primarily resulting from:</FONT></P>
<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: -7.1pt; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 12pt 
7.1pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 9pt" lang=EN-US color=black 
face=symbol>&#183;</FONT><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 7pt" lang=EN-US color=black 
face="times new roman">&nbsp; </FONT><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 9pt" lang=EN-US 
color=black face="arial narrow,sans-serif">Diesel (a 5% increase) &#8211; due to
seasonal demand to support summer grain seeding and industrial activity, as well
as higher consumption by thermoelectric plants;</FONT></P>
<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: -7.1pt; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 12pt 
7.1pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 9pt" lang=EN-US color=black 
face=symbol>&#183;</FONT><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 7pt" lang=EN-US color=black 
face="times new roman">&nbsp; </FONT><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 9pt" lang=EN-US 
color=black face="arial narrow,sans-serif">Fuel oil (an 11% increase) &#8211; 
due to higher consumption by thermoelectric plants; and</FONT></P>
<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: -7.1pt; MARGIN: 12pt 0cm 12pt 
7.1pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt" lang=EN-US color=black 
face=symbol>&#183;</FONT><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 7pt" lang=EN-US color=black 
face="times new roman">&nbsp; </FONT><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 9pt" lang=EN-US 
color=black face="arial narrow,sans-serif">LPG (a 4% increase) &#8211; due to 
the lower average temperatures and higher economic activity.</FONT></P></TD>
<TD style="PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; 
PADDING-TOP: 0cm" vAlign=top width="2%">
<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 6pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 
9pt" lang=EN-US face="arial narrow,sans-serif"></FONT>&nbsp;</P></TD>
<TD style="PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; 
PADDING-TOP: 0cm" vAlign=top width="49%">
<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 6pt"><B><FONT style="FONT-
SIZE: 9pt" lang=EN-US face="arial narrow,sans-serif">(Jan-Sep/2014 x Jan-
Sep/2013):</FONT></B><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 9pt" lang=EN-US face="arial 
narrow,sans-serif"> Our domestic sales volumes increased by 4% in Jan-Sep/2014 
when compared to Jan-Sep/2013, primarily resulting from:</FONT></P>
<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: -10pt; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 12pt 
10pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 9pt" lang=EN-US color=black 
face=symbol>&#183;</FONT><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 7pt" lang=EN-US color=black 
face="times new roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </FONT><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 9pt" 
lang=EN-US color=black face="arial narrow,sans-serif">Diesel (a 2% increase) 
&#8211; due to higher consumption by infrastructure construction work and an 
increase in the Brazilian diesel-fueled light vehicle fleet (vans, pick-ups and 
SUVs);</FONT></P>
<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: -10pt; MARGIN: 12pt 0cm 12pt 
10pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 9pt" lang=EN-US color=black 
face=symbol>&#183;</FONT><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 7pt" lang=EN-US color=black 
face="times new roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </FONT><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 9pt" 
lang=EN-US color=black face="arial narrow,sans-serif">Gasoline (a 5% increase) 
&#8211; due to an increase in the automotive fleet attributable to the 
competitive advantage of gasoline prices relatively to ethanol prices in most 
Brazilian states and to a higher household consumption. An increase in the 
anhydrous ethanol mandatory content in Type C gasoline from 20% to 25% partially
offset these effects; and</FONT></P>
<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: -10pt; MARGIN: 12pt 0cm 12pt 
10pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt" lang=EN-US color=black 
face=symbol>&#183;</FONT><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 7pt" lang=EN-US color=black 
face="times new roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </FONT><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 9pt" 
lang=EN-US color=black face="arial narrow,sans-serif">Fuel oil (a 21% increase) 
&#8211; higher demand by ancillary thermoelectric plants in several Brazilian 
states when compared to Jan-Sep/2013.</FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE></DIV>
<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt"><B><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 
11pt" lang=EN-US color=black face="arial narrow,sans-
serif"></FONT></B>&nbsp;</P>

<DIV align=center>
<TABLE style="BORDER-BOTTOM: medium none; BORDER-LEFT: medium none; WIDTH: 100%;
BORDER-TOP: medium none; BORDER-RIGHT: medium none" border=0 cellSpacing=0 
cellPadding=0>
<TR>
<TD style="PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; 
PADDING-TOP: 0cm" vAlign=top width="49%">
<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 6pt"><B><FONT style="FONT-
SIZE: 9pt" lang=EN-US face="arial narrow,sans-serif">(3Q-2014 x 2Q-
2014):</FONT></B><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 9pt" lang=EN-US face="arial 
narrow,sans-serif"> Crude oil exports were higher, due to an increase in crude 
oil production and to the realization of exports that were in transit on June 
30. </FONT></P>
<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 6pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 
9pt" lang=EN-US face="arial narrow,sans-serif">The decrease in crude oil imports
is attributable to the higher import volume in the 2Q-2014 attributable to 
economic signals of trading opportunities. </FONT></P></TD>
<TD style="PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; 
PADDING-TOP: 0cm" vAlign=top width="2%">
<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 6pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 
9pt" lang=EN-US face="arial narrow,sans-serif"></FONT>&nbsp;</P></TD>
<TD style="PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; 
PADDING-TOP: 0cm" vAlign=top width="49%">
<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 6pt"><B><FONT style="FONT-
SIZE: 9pt" lang=EN-US face="arial narrow,sans-serif">(Jan-Sep/2014 x Jan-
Sep/2013):</FONT></B><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 9pt" lang=EN-US face="arial 
narrow,sans-serif"> Crude oil exports and refining throughput were higher, 
resulting from an increase in crude oil production, which helped reduce crude 
oil imports. </FONT></P>
<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 6pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 
9pt" lang=EN-US face="arial narrow,sans-serif">Oil product imports were higher 
and oil product exports were lower in Jan-Sep/2014 when compared to Jan-Sep/2013
to meet an increase in domestic demand.</FONT></P>
<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 6pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 
9pt" lang=EN-US face="arial narrow,sans-
serif"></FONT>&nbsp;</P></TD></TR></TABLE></DIV>

color=black face="arial narrow,sans-serif"></FONT></B>&nbsp;</P>

<P style="BORDER-BOTTOM: medium none; TEXT-ALIGN: right; BORDER-LEFT: medium

<DIV align=center>
<TABLE style="BORDER-BOTTOM: medium none; BORDER-LEFT: medium none; WIDTH: 100%;
MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; BORDER-TOP: medium none; BORDER-RIGHT: medium none" border=0 
cellSpacing=0 cellPadding=0>
<TR>
<TD style="PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; 
PADDING-TOP: 0cm" vAlign=top width="48%">
<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 6pt"><B><FONT style="FONT-
SIZE: 9pt" lang=EN-US face="arial narrow,sans-serif">(3Q-2014 x 2Q-
2014):</FONT></B><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 9pt" lang=EN-US face="arial 
narrow,sans-serif"> Electricity sales volumes were 3% higher in the Free 
Contracting Environment &#8211; ACL due to seasonal long-term agreements and to 
higher sales volumes in the spot market.</FONT></P>
<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 6pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 
9pt" lang=EN-US face="arial narrow,sans-serif">Electricity sales volumes were 9%
higher in the Regulated Contracting Environment &#8211; ACR due to the full 
impact of the 574 average MW sold in the A0/2014 electricity auction, which was 
delivered as from May 2014. </FONT></P>
<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 6pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 
9pt" lang=EN-US face="arial narrow,sans-serif">The 2% increase in electricity 
generation is attributable to higher thermoelectric demand in August, setting a 
monthly record level for 2014, compared to a lower level in June, resulting from
higher rainfall levels in the Southern region of Brazil. </FONT></P>
<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 6pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 
9pt" lang=EN-US face="arial narrow,sans-serif">The 23% decrease in LNG imports 
was due to a higher supply of domestic natural gas attributable to an increase 
in natural gas production. </FONT></P>
<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 6pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 
9pt" lang=EN-US face="arial narrow,sans-serif">The 2% increase in natural gas 
imports from Bolivia was due to higher thermoelectric demand.</FONT></P></TD>
<TD style="PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; 
PADDING-TOP: 0cm" vAlign=top width="4%">
<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 6pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 
9pt" lang=EN-US face="arial narrow,sans-serif"></FONT>&nbsp;</P></TD>
<TD style="PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; 
PADDING-TOP: 0cm" vAlign=top width="48%">
<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 6pt"><B><FONT style="FONT-
SIZE: 9pt" lang=EN-US face="arial narrow,sans-serif">(Jan-Sep/2014 x Jan-
Sep/2013): </FONT></B><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 9pt" lang=EN-US face="arial 
narrow,sans-serif">Electricity sales volumes were 41% lower in Jan-Sep/2014 when
compared to Jan-Sep/2013 resulting from the shift of a portion of our available 
capacity (574 average MW) towards the regulated contracting environment in the 
domestic market (Regulated Contracting Environment &#8211; ACR). The termination
of our lease agreement for UTE Arauc&#225;ria, which reduced the availability of
electricity for trading (349 average MW) and the lower demand in the spot 
market, attributable to higher spot prices, also reduced our sales volumes. 
</FONT></P>
<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 6pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 
9pt" lang=EN-US face="arial narrow,sans-serif">Electricity generation was 4% 
higher and spot prices increased by 161% due to lower rainfall levels in the 
period. </FONT></P>
<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 6pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 
9pt" lang=EN-US face="arial narrow,sans-serif">LNG imports and natural gas 
imports from Bolivia were 25% and 5% higher, respectively, to meet a higher 
thermoelectric demand.</FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE></DIV>
<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0cm 0pt 0pt 0cm"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 
11pt" lang=EN-US color=black face="arial narrow,sans-serif"></FONT>&nbsp;</P>
<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0cm 0pt 0pt 0cm"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 
11pt" lang=EN-US color=black face="arial narrow,sans-serif"></FONT>&nbsp;</P>

<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 
11pt" lang=EN-US color=black face="arial narrow,sans-serif">Our consolidated net
debt in </FONT><I><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt" lang=EN-US color=black 
face="arial narrow,sans-serif">Reais</FONT></I><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt" 
lang=EN-US color=black face="arial narrow,sans-serif"> increased by 18% as of 
September 30, 2014, when compared to December 31, 2013, resulting from 
additional long-term financing and from the impact of the 4.6% depreciation of 
the </FONT><I><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt" lang=EN-US color=black face="arial 
narrow,sans-serif">Real</FONT></I><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt" lang=EN-US 
color=black face="arial narrow,sans-serif"> against the U.S. dollar. Net debt 
includes finance lease obligations of R$ 203 million as of September 30, 2014, 
and R$ 209 million as of December 31, 2013. </FONT></P>
<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 12pt 0cm"><FONT style="DISPLAY: 
none"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt" lang=PT-BR face="Times New 
Roman"></FONT></FONT>&nbsp;</P>
<P style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt" lang=PT-BR 
face="Times New Roman"></FONT>&nbsp;</P>
<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: right">7</P></DIV>
<HR align=center SIZE=2 width="100%" noShade>
<DIV style="PAGE-BREAK-BEFORE: always">&nbsp;</DIV>
&nbsp; <A name="page_8"></A>
<DIV style="PADDING-LEFT: 0%; PADDING-RIGHT: 0%">
<a name="_bclHeader8"></a><DIV>
<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; MARGIN: 12pt 0pt 0pt 0cm" align=center>
<IMG src="x14121222430100.jpg" width=794 height=169>&nbsp;</P>
<P style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 0pt">&nbsp;</P></DIV>
<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: avoid; TEXT-INDENT: -1cm; 
MARGIN: 12pt 0cm 12pt 1cm"><B><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt" lang=EN-US 
face="arial narrow,sans-serif"></FONT></B>&nbsp;</P>
<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: avoid; TEXT-INDENT: -1cm; 
MARGIN: 12pt 0cm 12pt 1cm"><B><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt" lang=EN-US 
face="arial narrow,sans-serif">Measures to improve corporate governance and 
internal controls</FONT></B></P>
<P style="BORDER-BOTTOM: medium none; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; BORDER-LEFT: medium 
none; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 12pt; BORDER-TOP: medium none; BORDER-RIGHT: medium 
none"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt" lang=EN-US face="arial narrow,sans-
serif">The Company has undertaken the following initiatives to improve its 
corporate governance system:</FONT></P>
<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: -14.2pt; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 12pt 
14.2pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt" lang=EN-US face=Calibri,sans-serif>-
</FONT><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 7pt" lang=EN-US face="times new 
roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </FONT><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt"
lang=EN-US face="arial narrow,sans-serif">on November 25, 2014 the Board of 
Directors approved the creation of the position of Executive Director of
Governance, Risk and Compliance, replacing the position of Executive Director of
the International business area, with the aim of supporting the Company&#8217;s 
compliance programs and to mitigate risks in its activities, including fraud and
corruption. The new Director will serve a three-year term and will only be 
removed if determined by the Board of Directors, with quorum including the vote 
of at least one Board Member elected by the minority or by the preferred 
shareholders. Before being presented to the Executive Board, matters regarding 
corporate governance, risk management and compliance shall be approved by the 
new Director. The Board of Directors will appoint the new Director from a list 
of three professionals, previously selected by an executive search firm. By the 
end of January, the new Director will have been appointed and will be 
undertaking its duties;</FONT></P>
<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: -14.2pt; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 12pt 
14.2pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt" lang=EN-US face=Calibri,sans-serif>-
</FONT><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 7pt" lang=EN-US face="times new 
roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </FONT><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt"
lang=EN-US face="arial narrow,sans-serif">the development and implementation, 
between 2012 and 2014, of 66 measures to improve corporate governance, risk 
management and control, which are documented in standards and minutes of 
management meetings that establish procedures, methods, responsibilities and 
other guidelines to integrate such measures into the Company&#8217;s 
practices;</FONT></P>
<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: -14.2pt; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 12pt 
14.2pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt" lang=EN-US face=Calibri,sans-serif>-
</FONT><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 7pt" lang=EN-US face="times new 
roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </FONT><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt"
lang=EN-US face="arial narrow,sans-serif">implemented changes in Company 
management as a result of the findings from the Internal Investigative 
Committees due to failures to comply with internal policies. It is important to 
note that the Company has not dismissed any personnel, because the reports from 
the Internal Investigative Committees have not yet provided evidence of 
fraudulent intent, bad faith or receipt of improper advantages with respect to 
the employees named therein.</FONT></P>
<P style="BORDER-BOTTOM: medium none; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; BORDER-LEFT: medium 
none; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 12pt; BORDER-TOP: medium none; BORDER-RIGHT: medium 
none"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt" lang=EN-US face="arial narrow,sans-
serif">The Company continues to assess the effectiveness of internal controls 
over financial reporting mainly considering the conclusions reached thus far by 
the Internal Investigative Committees, and any necessary changes to its control 
environment will be implemented.</FONT></P>
<P style="BORDER-BOTTOM: medium none; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; BORDER-LEFT: medium 
none; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 12pt; BORDER-TOP: medium none; BORDER-RIGHT: medium 
none"><FONT style="DISPLAY: none"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt" lang=PT-BR 
face="Times New Roman"></FONT></FONT>&nbsp;</P></DIV>
<P style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt" lang=PT-BR 
face="Times New Roman"></FONT>&nbsp;</P>
<P style="TEXT-ALIGN: right">8</P>
